 - AI systems can interpret and execute commands, leading to potential misuse without traditional security breaches.

Importance: 8

This highlights the urgent need for enhanced governance and verification processes in enterprise AI deployments to ensure actions are not executed without proper scrutiny.

 - AI systems are being integrated into various enterprise workflows, creating new vulnerabilities.

Category: Cybersecurity
Importance: 8
A vulnerability known as HollowByte allows unauthenticated attackers to cause a denial-of-service condition in OpenSSL servers using an 11-byte payload. This flaw, which has been addressed in recent versions of OpenSSL, can lead to significant memory depletion and operational disruptions in environments utilizing OpenSSL for secure communications. Organizations are advised to upgrade to patched versions to mitigate the risk of exploitation.

 - The HollowByte vulnerability affects OpenSSL servers, causing memory allocation issues.
 - Organizations using OpenSSL should prioritize updating to fixed versions to prevent potential attacks.

Source: https://www.bleepingcomputer.com/news/security/hollowbyte-ddos-flaw-bloats-openssl-server-memory-with-11-byte-payload/

---


Category: Cybersecurity
Importance: 8
A new Denial-of-Service vulnerability known as HollowByte affects OpenSSL servers, allowing attackers to exploit memory allocation issues using a small payload, effectively bloating server memory and causing operational disruptions. OpenSSL has issued a patch for this issue, which can impact various software projects relying on it, including popular web servers and database systems, and organizations are advised to upgrade their OpenSSL versions immediately to mitigate the risk.

 - HollowByte vulnerability allows unauthenticated attackers to cause Denial-of-Service on OpenSSL servers.
 - The vulnerability can severely impact memory allocation leading to operational disruptions.

Source: https://www.bleepingcomputer.com/news/security/hollowbyte-ddos-flaw-bloats-openssl-server-memory-with-11-byte-payload/

Criminal actors are increasingly using residential proxies as part of sophisticated identity simulation strategies in carding, recognizing that these proxies require a match with various identity signals for effective use. The once straightforward view of residential proxies as anonymity tools has shifted to a more complex understanding where authorities categorize proxies into 'clean' and 'dirty' based on their reputations and previous usage against financial services. This change reflects an evolving landscape in cybercrime, where precision and credibility in digital identities are becoming essential to evade fraud detection systems.

 - Residential proxies are integral to carding but are now analyzed based on their reputation and prior usage.
 - Carders are now seeking proxies that align with specific identity signals to create convincing digital personas.
 - The complexity of residential proxy usage illustrates the ongoing adaptation of cybercriminals to evade security measures.

Source: https://www.bleepingcomputer.com/news/security/inside-the-search-for-clean-residential-proxies-for-carding/

Importance: 7

There is a noted shift in the perception of residential proxies, which are now categorized into 'clean' and 'dirty' pools based on their usage history and reputation among fraudsters, complicating efforts to circumvent fraud detection mechanisms. The market for high-quality, finance-compatible residential proxies is growing, driven by restrictions from providers on accessing financial services.

 - Residential proxies are now part of a broader scheme for constructing digital identities in carding operations.

 - The demand for 'clean' residential IPs has led to a burgeoning market for providers offering finance-enabled services.

Despite this ruling invalidating China's claims, ASEAN states have struggled to effectively incorporate its principles into their diplomatic strategies, focusing instead on crisis management. Recent developments, like the Philippines’ upcoming chairmanship and efforts to strengthen regional maritime cooperation, suggest a shift towards greater unity and legal coherence among ASEAN members.

 - Southeast Asian governments are prioritizing crisis management over legal advocacy due to China's growing assertiveness.
 - The Philippines aims to reinforce the maritime Code of Conduct through a framework that includes UNCLOS and the Arbitration Award.

JPEG files can be structured to allow low-resolution previews while downloading, utilizing multiple scans for data representation. This technique has been adapted to concatenate multiple JPEGs into a single file, enabling creative data encoding techniques, such as embedding animations or even videos within one image file, albeit with limitations on playback timing and rendering options.

 - JPEG files have the option to save low frequency components first for partial display.
 - Multiple JPEGs can be concatenated to create single files capable of encoding animation.

Source: https://maurycyz.com/projects/bad_jpeg/

This technique enables multiple scans within a single JPEG file, allowing for a series of images or animations to be packed together, although with limitations on playback and timing due to network delays.

 - JPEGs can save image data in multiple scans to facilitate gradual rendering.

Importance: 8
Researchers have discovered the first atmosphere around an Earth-like rocky planet named LHS 1140b, located 48 light-years away from Earth, orbiting in the habitable zone of a distant star. This finding marks a significant step towards understanding the potential for life beyond our solar system, although only helium has been detected in the atmosphere so far, which does not support life on its own.

 - The atmosphere found around LHS 1140b is the first around a rocky, Earth-like planet in a habitable zone.
 - The discovery could indicate the existence of conditions suitable for life beyond our solar system.

Source: https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cy4kdd1e0ejo

Importance: 7
The Zilog Z80 processor, which was launched 50 years ago, has played a significant role in the development of early personal and embedded computing technology. Over the years, it established a de facto standard for 8-bit microcomputers, influencing software development and hardware design, and it was recently discontinued in June 2024 after its long-standing use in various applications.

 - The Zilog Z80 processor was launched in 1976 and became a standard for 8-bit microcomputers.
 - It was used in early personal computers and many industrial applications, playing a crucial role in software compatibility.
 - The Z80 was officially discontinued in June 2024 after a long period of use.

Source: https://goliath32.com/blog/z80.html

Category: Cybersecurity
Importance: 8
Multiple vulnerabilities have been identified in TP-Link's Kasa Spot EC71 indoor cameras, leading to potential risks including unauthorized access to user credentials and exposure of precise GPS data. These vulnerabilities have been patched in a recent firmware update, but the nature of the vulnerabilities suggests a pattern of targeted remediation rather than a comprehensive security review by the vendor.

 - Vulnerabilities in TP-Link Kasa Spot EC71 cameras include insecure credential storage and unauthenticated GPS exposure.
 - The vendor has released a patch to address these vulnerabilities, which were present for several years across different devices.

Source: https://github.com/BadChemical/IoT-Vulnerability-Research-Public/blob/main/TP-Link_Kasa_EC71/Kasa_EC71.md

---


Category: Cybersecurity
Importance: 8
Recent security research revealed multiple vulnerabilities in TP-Link's Kasa Spot EC71 cameras, including issues related to RSA key management, unsalted credential storage, and unauthorized GPS data exposure. These vulnerabilities, identified as CVE-2026-9770 and CVE-2026-13230, were patched in firmware version 2.4.1 following a coordinated disclosure process that lasted over six months. The flawed firmware allowed potential attackers to compromise user credentials and locate users' homes, creating serious security implications for consumers.

 - Researchers discovered serious vulnerabilities in TP-Link's Kasa Spot EC71 cameras, posing risks to user security.
 - The vulnerabilities included unsecured credential storage and unauthorized GPS data exposure.
 - TP-Link has released a patched firmware version to address these security flaws.

Source: https://github.com/BadChemical/IoT-Vulnerability-Research-Public/blob/main/TP-Link_Kasa_EC71/Kasa_EC71.md

Importance: 5
New advancements in data structure optimization show that static search trees, known as S-trees, can outperform traditional binary search by as much as 40 times in throughput when querying sorted data. Techniques including multi-threading, batching, and auto-vectorization optimize these tree structures for applications like genomic indexing where efficient data retrieval is crucial.

 - Static search trees (S-trees) provide enhanced performance over binary search by optimizing query throughput.
 - Innovative methods such as multi-threading and SIMD instructions dramatically improve data structure efficiency for high-demand applications like genome indexing.

Source: https://curiouscoding.nl/posts/static-search-tree/

---


Category: Technology
Importance: 8
Recent advancements in computer science, specifically in data structure optimization, have led to the creation of static search trees, which can perform searches significantly faster than traditional binary search methods. These new approaches leverage various data layouts and multi-threading to enhance throughput, especially useful for high-volume data sets such as genome indexing. Researchers are also exploring auto-vectorization and SIMD instructions to further improve performance.

 - Static search trees provide up to 40 times faster search capabilities compared to binary search.
 - Implementations focus on optimizing throughput through innovative coding techniques and hardware utilization.

Source: https://curiouscoding.nl/posts/static-search-tree/

Union Pacific Railroad is implementing a new method to manage heat-related track conditions by applying white paint to rails, which reflects sunlight and lowers surface temperatures by approximately 20 degrees. This initiative is part of a broader strategy to enhance safety and reduce derailment incidents in extreme heat conditions, utilizing techniques adapted from European rail systems. As the largest freight railroad in the U.S., Union Pacific plays a critical role in the national supply chain, servicing a vast network of communities and industries across 23 states.

 - Union Pacific is applying white paint to railroad tracks to mitigate heat-related expansion issues.
 - The initiative aims to improve safety and reduce derailment incidents, reflecting ongoing efforts in operational excellence.
 - Union Pacific plays a vital role in the U.S. supply chain by connecting numerous communities through its extensive rail network.

Source: https://www.up.com/news/safety/Tracking-Rail-Heat-260608

Category: Other
Importance: 4
Individuals and organizations often respond to problems in three key ways: by pushing problems around rather than resolving them, by preserving issues for personal or institutional benefit, and by inadvertently creating new problems when attempting to solve existing ones. Understanding these responses can inform better problem-solving approaches and facilitate greater awareness of underlying motives and incentives in organizational dynamics.

 - People often shift problems around instead of resolving them, leading to inefficiencies.
 - Some individuals or institutions may maintain problems to uphold their relevance or benefits.
 - Solving one problem may lead to the emergence of new issues, necessitating a careful evaluation of solutions.

Source: https://improvesomething.today/responses-to-problems/

---


Category: Business
Importance: 4
Organizations often respond to problems in ways that do not involve direct resolution, leading to practices such as shifting issues around, maintaining problems to justify their roles, or unintentionally creating new problems. These responses can hinder progress and require a broader understanding of the systems and incentives at play. Acknowledging and addressing these patterns is critical for effective problem-solving.

 - Organizations frequently push problems around instead of resolving them.
 - Some entities may preserve existing issues to maintain their relevance.
 - Solving one problem often leads to the emergence of another.

Source: https://improvesomething.today/responses-to-problems/

Microsoft will stop providing updates, fixes, or security patches for OneDrive on Windows 10 versions prior to 22H2 after August 15, 2025.  - Microsoft is ending OneDrive sync support for Windows 10 versions before 22H2.
 - Users must upgrade to continue receiving updates or switch to a web interface.

The Australian government has expressed frustration over Laos' decision to pursue only minor charges related to the deaths of six backpackers, including two Australians, who died after consuming methanol-laced alcohol. This has prompted Australia to summon Laos' ambassador and appoint a special envoy to address the situation, as families of the victims demand more serious accountability for the tragedy.

 - Laos plans to press charges carrying a maximum penalty of one year in jail and a fine against those responsible for the deaths.
 - The Australian government is seeking to intervene and ensure that justice is served for the deceased, expressing disappointment over the expected leniency of the charges.

Source: https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cy5d4z343wlo?at_medium=RSS&at_campaign=rss

Importance: 5
Taco Bell is removing lettuce from its menu in certain states due to a link to a cyclosporiasis outbreak, which has infected over 1,600 people. The Centers for Disease Control and Prevention and the Food and Drug Administration are involved in tracing the outbreak back to a supplier in Mexico, and no deaths have been reported but several hospitalizations occurred due to the infection.

 - Taco Bell is taking precautionary measures by removing lettuce from its menu in specific states.
 - The outbreak has been traced to a supplier in Mexico and has resulted in significant health impacts.

Source: https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cm2gnglyv0jo?at_medium=RSS&at_campaign=rss

Category: Business
Importance: 7
Taco Bell is removing lettuce from its menu in certain states due to a link to an outbreak of cyclosporiasis, a parasitic infection that has affected 1,645 individuals across five states. The FDA has traced the outbreak to a supplier in Mexico, and while no fatalities have been reported, 94 hospitalization cases have occurred since the infections were first identified on May 13.

 - Taco Bell has taken precautionary measures to remove potentially contaminated lettuce from its affected locations.
 - The CDC and FDA are investigating a widespread outbreak of cyclosporiasis linked to a supplier in Mexico.

Importance: 8
In southern Ecuador, a high number of people with Laron syndrome, a rare genetic condition, have been found to have lower incidences of cancer and diabetes compared to the general population. Researchers are studying the genetic mutation to potentially develop treatments that could aid in cancer prevention and understand the mechanisms behind these health benefits.

 - Laron syndrome leads to a distinct genetic mutation affecting growth hormone receptors.
 - Research suggests lower levels of Insulin-like Growth Factor 1 (IGF-1) in Laron syndrome patients might contribute to reduced cancer rates.

Source: https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/c8jnlmek8reo?at_medium=RSS&at_campaign=rss

Importance: 7

Researchers are studying this genetic condition to understand its potential for developing treatments to prevent cancer. While there are ongoing efforts to explore the relationship between growth hormones and disease resistance, accessibility to treatment remains an issue for affected children.

 - Laron syndrome is characterized by short stature and results from a mutation that affects growth hormone receptors.
 - Research indicates that individuals with Laron syndrome exhibit significantly lower rates of cancer and diabetes, prompting scientific interest in their genetic condition for potential medical advances.

Category: Geopolitics
Importance: 10
The Chernobyl disaster in 1986 was caused by a catastrophic explosion in Reactor No. 4 of the nuclear power plant, which resulted from design flaws that were intentionally concealed by Soviet authorities. The deception surrounding the disaster had far-reaching consequences, contributing to public distrust and playing a significant role in the eventual collapse of the Soviet Union.

 - The Chernobyl disaster was one of the largest man-made nuclear disasters in history, leading to widespread radiation exposure.
 - The Soviet government's concealment of critical reactor design flaws contributed to the disaster and ultimately eroded public trust in the state.

Source: https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/europe/quote-of-the-day-by-valery-legasov-every-lie-we-tell-incurs-a-debt-to-the-truth-sooner-or-later-that-debt-is-paid-and-how-continuous-deception-led-to-the-chernobyl-disaster-in-1986-and-eventually-contributed-to-the-fall-of-the-ussr/articleshow/132469003.cms

Importance: 8
An international team of scientists has identified over 64,000 square miles of heat-resistant coral reefs across 71 countries, which are crucial for marine life amid a severe global bleaching crisis. The research utilized artificial intelligence to locate areas that could potentially safeguard corals from extreme heat and promote their recovery, offering a targeted approach for conservation efforts. This discovery arrives as more than 80% of the world's reefs have experienced bleaching-level heat since 2023, marking an unprecedented crisis for ocean ecosystems.

 - The study reveals significant areas of heat-resistant coral reefs that can aid in protecting marine ecosystems.
 - Research indicates that targeted conservation strategies can be developed based on these newly discovered coral sanctuaries.

Source: https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/science/scientists-discover-64000-square-miles-of-heat-resistant-coral-reefs-across-71-countries-that-could-help-protect-the-worlds-oceans-for-decades/articleshow/132466800.cms

In the business world, success is increasingly defined by the ability to create something genuinely new rather than merely imitating existing models. Entrepreneurs are encouraged to pursue innovation in areas that are not yet saturated with competition, particularly in transformative fields like artificial intelligence, healthcare, and education, where unique solutions are essential for standing out.

 - Successful businesses require a unique selling proposition that differentiates them from competitors.
 - Innovation in untouched markets is more likely to lead to substantial success than replicating existing successful models.

 - Scientists utilized DNA analysis to confirm the existence of the Himalayan pangolin, a species overlooked for nearly 200 years.
 - This discovery suggests the need for targeted conservation strategies as each pangolin species has different threats and genetic profiles.
 - The reclassification will influence how conservation and protection efforts are planned for this and other pangolin species.

This transaction transformed the residence into Cartier's American flagship store, solidifying its status as a prime luxury location, while the value dynamics of both the necklace and the mansion experienced contrasting trends over time.

 - Pierre Cartier secured a prominent Fifth Avenue mansion through a unique trade involving a rare pearl necklace.
 - The exchange marked a strategic move for Cartier, strengthening its brand presence in the American luxury market.
 - Over time, the value of the mansion increased significantly, while the value of the pearl necklace declined due to market changes.

Category: Geopolitics
Importance: 5
The Supreme Court has largely avoided addressing three significant constitutional provisions: the 13th Amendment's exception clause related to involuntary servitude, the guarantee clause of Article IV concerning republican governance, and the Third Amendment regarding the quartering of soldiers. These provisions have remained largely dormant in judicial interpretation, raising questions about their relevance and application in contemporary legal issues.

 - The 13th Amendment's exception clause allows for involuntary servitude as a punishment for a crime, which has led to legal debates and interpretations regarding forced labor in the U.S. justice system.
 - The guarantee clause of Article IV is often considered non-justiciable, giving courts little power to intervene in state governance issues.
 - The Third Amendment has seen minimal judicial scrutiny, leading to discussions about the contemporary implications of military and police presence in civilian life.

Source: https://www.scotusblog.com/2026/07/three-profound-constitutional-provisions-and-how-the-supreme-court-has-avoided-dealing-with-them/

---


Category: Geopolitics
Importance: 6
Discussions surrounding lesser-known provisions of the U.S. Constitution are gaining attention, particularly regarding the 13th Amendment's exception clause, which allows for involuntary servitude as a punishment for crime. Additionally, debates are arising about the judicial role in interpreting the guarantee clause of Article IV and the Third Amendment, both of which have seen limited court engagement over time. Legislative efforts are underway in some states to remove the exception clause from their constitutions, signaling a potential shift in the legal landscape.

 - The 13th Amendment's exception clause permits involuntary servitude for convicted criminals.
 - The guarantee clause of Article IV and the Third Amendment have been largely absent from judicial interpretation, raising questions about their relevance today.
 - Certain states are actively pursuing amendments to remove the exception clause, indicating a movement towards reevaluating historical constitutional provisions.

Source: https://www.scotusblog.com/2026/07/three-profound-constitutional-provisions-and-how-the-supreme-court-has-avoided-dealing-with-them/

Category: Other
Importance: 7
Astronomers have discovered the sugar erythritol in interstellar space near the center of the Milky Way, suggesting complex organic molecules essential for life can form in such environments before the birth of stars and planets. This finding raises the possibility that other life-supporting molecules may also be present in the cosmos, potentially contributing to the origins of life on planets like Earth. The discovery was made using radiotelescopes to study a molecular cloud known as G+0.693-0.027.

 - Erythritol, a sugar important for energy and biological structures, was found in interstellar space.
 - The discovery suggests that complex organic molecules could form before star and planet formation.
 - Scientists believe that sugars may have been delivered to Earth through asteroids and comets.

Source: https://www.mk.ru/science/2026/07/18/obnaruzhennyy-v-mezhzvezdnom-prostranstve-sakhar-nazvan-klyuchom-k-razgadke-proiskhozhdeniya-zhizni.html

---


Category: Other
Importance: 8
Astronomers have discovered a sugar called erythritol in the interstellar medium near the center of the Milky Way galaxy, suggesting that key compounds for life may form in the vast spaces between stars. This finding indicates that relatively complex sugars can be synthesized in the interstellar medium prior to the formation of stars and planets, with the potential for other important molecules for life's origin to be identified in space. It is estimated that between 0.5 to 50 million metric tons of this sugar could have reached Earth's surface during the Late Heavy Bombardment, a period approximately 4 billion years ago.

 - Erythritol, a sugar key to life's building blocks, has been detected in interstellar clouds.
 - The discovery implies the potential for complex organic molecules to form in space before planetary formation.
 - Research indicates significant amounts of these sugars could have reached Earth through asteroids during the Late Heavy Bombardment.

Source: https://www.mk.ru/science/2026/07/18/obnaruzhennyy-v-mezhzvezdnom-prostranstve-sakhar-nazvan-klyuchom-k-razgadke-proiskhozhdeniya-zhizni.html

Importance: 5
Sleep deprivation can have serious negative effects on cognitive performance and overall health. The military defines total sleep deprivation as being awake for 24 hours, with chronic partial sleep deprivation resulting from consistently getting less than seven hours of sleep each night. Hallucinations, emotional exhaustion, and increased risk of mental health issues are associated with extreme sleep deprivation.

 - Total sleep deprivation is defined as being awake for 24 hours.
 - Chronic partial sleep deprivation leads to diminished cognitive performance and health risks.
 - Hallucinations and emotional exhaustion can occur from prolonged periods without sleep.

Source: https://lifehacker.com/how-long-can-you-go-without-sleep?utm_medium=RSS

Importance: 5
Extreme sleep deprivation has been studied for its effects on health and cognitive performance, showing significant impairment after 24 hours without sleep. Records of prolonged wakefulness have occurred, with the Guinness Book of World Records ceasing to monitor due to health risks. Recommendations for maintaining sleep quality include ensuring adequate rest periods and addressing insomnia through professional evaluation.

 - Extreme sleep deprivation can lead to serious impairments in cognitive function.
 - The military recommends allowing soldiers eight hours of sleep per 24-hour period to maintain performance.
 - Chronic sleep deprivation is linked to various health issues, including increased anxiety and depression.

The Federal Energy Regulatory Commission (FERC) has indicated a need for urgent reforms within PJM to address the ongoing challenges in the power grid management and to facilitate timely responses to the energy demands of the region.

 - PJM's capacity auction results indicate a troubling shortfall in power supply.
 - FERC is advocating for immediate reforms to improve the efficiency and reliability of the energy grid.

Source: https://www.zerohedge.com/energy/pjm-capacity-auction-results-compound-alarm-bells-ferc-chairman-swett

---


Category: Geopolitics
Importance: 7
PJM Interconnection's recent capacity auction resulted in a significant shortfall, clearing nearly 7 GW below its reliability target and only attracting about 500 MW of new power supply. Federal Energy Regulatory Commission (FERC) Chairman Laura Swett indicated that this outcome highlights the need for systemic reforms at PJM and called for immediate action from all stakeholders involved to address the complex issues impacting the region's energy grid stability.

 - PJM's capacity auction results fell significantly short of reliability targets.
 - FERC emphasizes the need for urgent reforms and collaboration among various stakeholders.

Source: https://www.zerohedge.com/energy/pjm-capacity-auction-results-compound-alarm-bells-ferc-chairman-swett

Category: Business
Importance: 8
Apple is in early settlement discussions with the U.S. Department of Justice regarding a 2024 antitrust lawsuit accusing the company of maintaining a monopoly in the smartphone market. The lawsuit, filed by the government under the Biden administration, alleges that Apple's practices hinder competition and harm developers and consumers. Changes made by Apple since the lawsuit was filed include support for RCS messaging and allowing cloud gaming apps on the App Store.

 - Apple is negotiating a settlement over antitrust allegations involving its market practices.
 - The lawsuit claims that Apple has made it difficult for competitors and consumers due to its dominant position.

Source: https://www.zerohedge.com/markets/apple-and-doj-early-settlement-talks-over-2024-antitrust-lawsuit

Importance: 4
U.S. Navy Blue Angels pilots conducted a low-altitude flight maneuver over a crowd in Pensacola Beach, Florida, during an air show event. The incident raised questions about safety protocols, but the Secretary of the Navy stated that there would be no reprimands for the pilots involved. No injuries were reported, and the Blue Angels plan to continue their performances as scheduled.

 - The Blue Angels are celebrating their 80th anniversary with air shows featuring precision maneuvers.
 - The Navy is conducting a review of the low-altitude maneuver while maintaining that safety is a top priority.

Category: Business
Importance: 8
Elon Musk has acquired a Jacksonville-based power company, New APR Energy, for around $1 billion, which specializes in mobile gas-turbine power generation. This acquisition aims to support energy needs for Musk's AI ventures and data centers, providing flexible energy solutions amid challenges with grid power. New APR Energy operates a fleet capable of generating over 1 gigawatt of power and can rapidly deploy its turbines in various locations.

 - Musk's acquisition of New APR Energy illustrates a strategic move to enhance energy supply for his tech projects.
 - The company has a proven track record of delivering rapid mobile power solutions, which aligns with Musk's business needs.

Source: https://www.zerohedge.com/energy/musk-buys-florida-based-energy-company

---


Category: Business
Importance: 7
Elon Musk has acquired New APR Energy, a Florida-based mobile gas-turbine provider, for approximately $1 billion to address energy needs for his data centers. The company operates a fleet capable of generating over 1 gigawatt of power, which can be deployed quickly for disaster response. This purchase marks Musk's continued investment in the energy sector, building on his previous investment in SolarCity and his ongoing work with artificial intelligence.

 - Musk's acquisition aims to secure energy solutions for his data centers.
 - New APR Energy has the capability to generate sufficient power for 750,000 homes and can deploy turbines rapidly.

Source: https://www.zerohedge.com/energy/musk-buys-florida-based-energy-company
